 Mulayam Singh Yadav to remain the national president, Akhilesh withdraw his claim
 2

 cycle to ab akhilesh kii: naresh agarwalsapa main akhilesh gut ke netaa naresh agarwal ne aaj tak ke saath khaas baatcheet main kaha ki cycle to ab akhilesh kii he

 yah do alag-alag cycle desh main bah rahi do vichaardhaara ko darshaati he

 ab kiranmay nanda ke is bayaan se maamle ne nayaa mode le liya he
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi announced on Sunday that the controversial system of taxation from the previous date in the country is now a thing of the past and this chapter will not be reopened in India
 piem modi kaa yah bayaan sthir kar pranali ko lekar videshi niveshkon kii chintaaen dur karne ke uddeshy se aayaa he

 pradhanmantri ne kaha ki unki sarkaar yah sunishchit karnaa chaahati he ki videshi niveshak bharat main aagaamee 15 saal tak kii kar pranali ko lekar spasht rahe

 sarkaar yah bharosa sunishchit karne ke liye anek kadam uthaa rahi he
 This government is known for stable and predictable tax system
 is sandarbh main unhone 2012 main iskar kanoon main sanshodhan ke jariye lagu kii gai pichhali taarikh se kar vyavastha kaa sandarbh diya

 piem modi ne bharat-france vyapaar shikhar sammelan main kaha, pichhali taarikh se karadhaan beeti baat ho gai
 That chapter will no longer reopen
 ham yah sunishchit kar rahe hai ki us adhyay ko na to yah sarkaar or na hi bhavi sarkarein khol saken
